Only the owner of the channel can upload videos to their YouTube account and they cannot delegate the task to someone else in the team.</p> \n<p>Google Drive has the concept of shared folders. A folder can have multiple collaborators and anyone can upload files to that folder. Wouldn’t it be useful if such a feature were available for YouTube channels as well? You maintain a single YouTube account and multiple people can upload videos to your common account without the owner having to share their Google account credentials with anyone.</p> \n<p><span \n<p>Introducing YouTube Uploader, a simple file upload form that lets anyone upload videos to your YouTube channel from their desktop or mobile phone.</p> \n<p>The user who is uploading the video doesn’t even need a Google account and they’ll still be able to upload video files of any size to your YouTube channel via a simple online form. Once the video file is uploaded, YouTube will take a minute or two to process the video and, depending on your privacy setting, it will go live on the YouTube channel.</p> \n<h3 id=\"make-your-own-youtube-uploader\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/internet/youtube-uploader/29161/#make-your-own-youtube-uploader\" aria-label=\"make your own youtube uploader permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>Make your Own YouTube Uploader</h3> \n<p>If you have a collaborative YouTube channel with multiple contributors, you may consider setting up your own private YouTube Uploader form and any of the contributors will be able to upload their work on your channel directly via the form.</p> \n<p><iframe width=\"100%\" height=\"315\" src=\"https://www.youtube-nocookie.com/embed/PDB2-17f_kc?rel=0\" frameBorder=\"0\" allow=\"accelerometer; autoplay; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture\" allowfullscreen=\"\"></iframe></p> \n<p>Here’s how you can build a YouTube uploader for your team in <strong>3 easy steps</strong>.</p> \n<p><strong>Step 1:</strong> <a href=\"https://script.google.com/a/labnol.org/d/1E8gwvrfd_oFWfG28TLXWhEkOaHZBIaj28YXLe7MuYLxf1RQzd4be5ePl/edit?newcopy=true\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">Click here</a> to make a copy of the YouTube uploader script in your Google Drive.</p> \n<p>An active YouTube channel must be associated with the Google Account where you are copying the script. It is recommended that you create a new Google account to test the YouTube uploader script and create a channel for that account.</p> \n<p><strong>Step 2:</strong> Inside the Google Script editor, go to the Publish menu, choose Deploy as Web App and click Update.</p> \n<p><strong>Step 3:</strong> You’ll be presented with an <a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/internet/youtube-uploader/29161/youtube-permissions.png\">authorization screen</a> as the script needs permission to upload videos to your YouTube channel. It also needs permission to send email notifications when a new video is uploaded. Click the Allow button.</p> \n<p>That’s it. You’ll be presented with a video upload URL that you can share with your team members.</p> \n<p>When any user clicks the URL, a simple web form opens where they can fill in the video title, description, the video category, and the privacy mode (the YouTube video can be private,&nbsp;public or unlisted).</p> \n<p>All they have to do is select a video file from the desktop and click “Upload” to&nbsp;send the video to your YouTube channel directly.</p> \n<p><span class=\"gatsby-resp-image-wrapper\" Next, drag the yellow “Pegman” to any area on the Google Map to switch from aerial to street view. class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 collection of essential Mac Apps includes mostly lesser-known apps so the popular ones — like Evernote, Dropbox, Skype, OneNote, or Google Drive — aren’t listed here. Also, all the apps here are compatible with Yosemite and Catalina, the current version of Mac OS.</p> \n<p>Wherever possible, I have included the Mac App Store links because the store not only makes it easy for you to install apps on your Mac but, in the case of paid apps, you also have an option for <a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/software/mac-app-store-refund-purchase/28774/\">requesting refunds</a>.</p> \n<p>Let’s get started.</p> \n<ol> \n <li><p><a href=\"https://magnet.crowdcafe.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">Magnet</a> - A perfect windows management app for Mac that lets you move and <a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/software/resize-mac-windows-to-specific-size/28345/\">resize windows</a> with configurable keyboard shortcuts. You can move windows between multiple displays too. Another alternative is <a href=\"https://rectangleapp.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">Rectangle</a>.</p></li> \n <li><p><a href=\"https://imageoptim.com/mac\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">ImageOptim</a> - Always run your images through ImageOptim before uploading them on to your website. The Mac app will crush the size of your&nbsp;image files without affecting the visual quality.</p></li> \n <li><p><a href=\"https://apps.apple.com/in/app/hiddenme-hide-desktop-icons/id467040476?mt=12\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">HiddenMe</a> - If your Mac desktop is cluttered with folders and files, you can hide all the icons with a single click or with a keyboard shortcut.</p></li> \n <li><p><a href=\"https://itunes.apple.com/in/app/sitesucker/id442168834?mt=12\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">Site Sucker</a> - Download entire websites includes images, PDF files and mirror them on your local disk for offline browsing. Like <a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/software/wget-command-examples/28750/\">wget</a> but with a visual interface.</p></li> \n <li><p><a href=\"https://freemacsoft.net/appcleaner/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">App Cleaner</a> - The best uninstaller for your Mac that will automatically remove all the extra files that are left on the disk when you delete an app.</p></li> \n <li><p><a href=\"https://maccy.app/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">Maccy</a> - A clipboard manager that stores all that you copy to the clipboard and lets you paste the copied snippets into other apps with a simple shortcut. [CopyClip] is a good alternative.</p></li> \n <li><p><a href=\"https://github.com/Kevin-De-Koninck/Clean-Me\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">Clean Me</a> - Recover space on your Mac by deleting all the system logs, cache and other temp files that your Mac can easily do away with.</p></li> \n <li><p><a href=\"https://github.com/Mortennn/Dozer\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">Dozer</a> - An excellent alternative to the popular <a href=\"http://www.macbartender.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">Bartender</a> app. You can quickly re-order or even hide the app icons appearing in the Mac menu bar.</p></li> \n <li><p><a href=\"https://ranchero.com/netnewswire/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">NetNewsWire</a> - A clean and fast RSS Reader for your MacOS. We have an <a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/rss.xml\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">RSS Feed</a> too!</p></li> \n <li><p><a href=\"https://apps.apple.com/in/app/rss-bot-news-notifier/id605732865?mt=12\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">RSS Bot</a> - Access your RSS from your Mac’s menu bar and get notifications when new items are available. You can also apply filters to only show articles that match certain keywords.</p></li> \n</ol> \n<p><span class=\"gatsby-resp-image-wrapper\" style=\"position:relative;display:block;margin-left:auto;margin-right:auto;max-width:720px\"> <a class=\"gatsby-resp-image-link\" href=\"https://www.labnol.org/static/0ba75bae48bb86ed4e7362afb594b18f/56544/calculator.png\" style=\"display:block\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\"> <span class=\"gatsby-resp-image-background-image\" style=\"padding-bottom:61.11111111111111%;position:relative;bottom:0;left:0;display:block\"></span> <img class=\"gatsby-resp-image-image\" alt=\"Numi.app - The Smart Mac Calculator\" title=\"Numi.app - The Smart Mac Calculator\" src=\"https://www.labnol.org/static/0ba75bae48bb86ed4e7362afb594b18f/16546/calculator.png\" srcSet=\"/static/0ba75bae48bb86ed4e7362afb594b18f/96042/calculator.png 180w,/static/0ba75bae48bb86ed4e7362afb594b18f/7a322/calculator.png 360w,/static/0ba75bae48bb86ed4e7362afb594b18f/16546/calculator.png 720w,/static/0ba75bae48bb86ed4e7362afb594b18f/56544/calculator.png 778w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 720px) 100vw, 720px\" style=\"width:100%;height:100%;margin:0;vertical-align:middle;position:absolute;top:0;left:0\" loading=\"lazy\" /> </a> </span></p> \n<ol start=\"11\"> \n <li><p><a href=\"https://flotato.com\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">Flotato</a> - It turns any web page into a native Mac app that you can quickly open outside the web browser. Also see, <a href=\"http://fluidapp.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">Fluid</a>.</p></li> \n <li><p><a href=\"https://max.codes/latest/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">Latest</a> - It scans the Applications folder of your Mac and checks if all your installed apps are up to date. You can also update your outdated apps. <a href=\"https://www.corecode.io/macupdater/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">MacUpdater</a> is an even more powerful but paid alternative.</p></li> \n <li><p><a href=\"https://www.titanium-software.fr/en/onyx.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">Onyx</a> - Perform system maintenance tasks to improve the performance of your Mac, verify disks and more.</p></li> \n <li><p><a href=\"http://www.bresink.com/osx/TinkerTool.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">TinkerTool</a> - It provides access to several configuration settings that are otherwise hidden on the Mac. For instance, you can specify the default folder where Screenshots should be saved on the Mac.</p></li> \n <li><p><a href=\"https://github.com/newmarcel/KeepingYouAwake\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">KeepingYouAwake</a> - It keeps your Mac stay awake and also prevents your screen from going to sleep. If you need more features, use <a href=\"https://apps.apple.com/app/amphetamine/id937984704?mt=12\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">Amphetamine</a>.</p></li> \n <li><p><a href=\"https://shifty.natethompson.io/en/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">Shifty</a> - Easily toggle between dark and light mode on your Mac. You can also decide which of your Apps or websites should stay light, while your system runs in Dark Mode. Also see, <a href=\"https://nightowl.kramser.xyz/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">NightOwl</a>.</p></li> \n <li><p><a href=\"https://iina.io/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">IINA</a> - A modern alternative to the VLC Media Player that includes support for gestures and the touch bar in newer Macs.</p></li> \n <li><p><a href=\"https://bahoom.com/hyperswitch\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">HyperSwitch</a> - An improved window switching app for Mac that upgrades your default Command + Tab experience when cycling between open app windows.</p></li> \n <li><p><a href=\"http://richsomerfield.com/apps/textbar/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">TextBar</a> - You can specify <a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/software/linux-commands/19028/\">system commands</a> and the app will add the text output of those commands to the menu bar. For instance, <code class=\"language-text\">ipconfig getifaddr en0</code> will print your current IP address. You can also have these as desktop widgets with <a href=\"http://tracesof.net/uebersicht/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">Übersicht</a>.</p></li> \n <li><p><a href=\"https://tyke.app/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">Tyke</a> - A minimalistic notepad app that sits in the menu bar and lets you save quick notes.</p></li> \n</ol> you can use them to create impressive pixel paintings in minutes.</p> \n<p>Marina and Mallory <a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=eTjjhLi0Xtk\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">created</a> a bright and beautiful&nbsp;wall mural&nbsp;using&nbsp;Google Sheets. Japanese artist <a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OrwBc6PwAcY\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">Tatsuo Horiuchi</a> uses Microsoft Excel to draw masterpieces.</p> \n<p>The idea is simple. Each cell in the spreadsheet corresponds to a pixel in the painting. You find the color of the pixel and set that as the&nbsp;background color of&nbsp;the corresponding cell in the sheet. Now resize the cells in small perfect squares and your spreadsheet will resemble the original artwork.</p> \n<h2 id=\"how-to-paint-with-google-spreadsheets\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/software/turn-images-into-pixel-art/12978/#how-to-paint-with-google-spreadsheets\" aria-label=\"how to paint with google spreadsheets permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>How to Paint with Google Spreadsheets</h2> \n<p>If you would like to&nbsp;create your own spreadsheet art but don’t have the time&nbsp;to carefully paint every cell manually, here’s a simple workaround&nbsp;for you.&nbsp;You can take any photograph, vector art, GIF, or any other image and use Google Sheets to convert that bitmap image into spreadsheet art.</p> \n<p>Here’s some artwork created with Google Spreadsheets.</p> \n<p><img src=\"https://www.labnol.org/images/2008/pixel-painting.png\" alt=\"Pixel Painting\" /></p> \n<p><img src=\"https://www.labnol.org/images/2008/emoji-painting.png\" alt=\"Emoji Painting\" /></p> \n<p><img src=\"https://www.labnol.org/images/2008/emoji-art.jpg\" alt=\"Emoji Art\" /></p> \n<p>Watch the&nbsp;<strong><a href=\"https://youtu.be/hoHvxbKDO00\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">video tutorial</a></strong>&nbsp;or open this <strong><a href=\"http://bit.ly/MadeWithGoogleSheets\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">Google Sheet</a></strong>&nbsp;to explore more artwork made with Google Sheets. You can increase the zoom to view individual pixels.</p> \n<h3 id=\"create-pixel-art-with-google-sheets\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/software/turn-images-into-pixel-art/12978/#create-pixel-art-with-google-sheets\" aria-label=\"create pixel art with google sheets permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>Create Pixel Art with Google Sheets</h3> \n<p>It takes three easy steps to make pixel art with Google Sheets.</p> \n<ol> \n <li>Install <a href=\"https://gsuite.google.com/marketplace/app/appname/881112366576\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">Pixel Art</a> for Google Sheets.</li> \n <li>Type <code class=\"language-text\">sheets.new</code> in the browser to create a new Google Sheet. Go to Add-ons menu, choose Pixel Art and then select Open.</li> \n <li>Upload any image from your desktop, hit the Draw button and watch as your sheet magically transforms into beautiful art.</li> \n</ol> \n<p>Check this <a href=\"http://bit.ly/MadeWithGoogleSheets\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">Google Sheet</a> for more examples.</p> \n<h4 id=\"how-pixel-art-works\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/software/turn-images-into-pixel-art/12978/#how-pixel-art-works\" aria-label=\"how pixel art works permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>How Pixel Art Works?</h4> \n<p>The underlying&nbsp;<a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/code/19848-google-spreadsheets-colors\">Google Script</a>&nbsp;will now parse every single&nbsp;pixel of your&nbsp;image and write the corresponding <a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/internet/design/web-colors-in-hexadecimal/5456/\">hex color codes</a> in the cells of the spreadsheet.</p> \n<p>It will then set the background color of every cell as the color of the corresponding pixel in the uploaded image. If you have chosen the ‘emoji’ option, the cell will be filled with the closest emoji that matches the color of the pixel.</p> \n<p>In the last step, the Google Script will resize the cells and turn them into perfect squares. That’s it. Your spreadsheet art is now ready.</p> \n<div link=\"https://gsuite.google.com/marketplace/app/appname/881112366576\">\n  Download Pixel Art \n</div> \n<p>If you choose to transform your picture into emojis pixels, the script takes the average color of the pixel, finds the closest emoji and adds it to the corresponding cell in the sheet. The emoji module is based on the work of <a href=\"https://github.com/notwaldorf/emojillate\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">Monica Dinculescu</a>.</p> \n<p><iframe width=\"100%\" height=\"315\" src=\"https://www.youtube-nocookie.com/embed/hoHvxbKDO00?rel=0\" frameBorder=\"0\" allow=\"accelerometer; autoplay; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture\" allowfullscreen=\"\"></iframe></p>","descriptionType":"html","publishedDate":"Wed, 27 May 2020 09:00:37 +0000","feedId":259,"bgimg":"https://www.labnol.org/images/2008/pixel-painting.png","linkMd5":"10f246e4043be4d47c46f34effd894a1","bgimgJsdelivr":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx12/cdn85@2020_5/2020/08/17/16-46-08-883_7710c2170c2c649c.webp","destWidth":1209,"destHeight":1086,"author":"","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://www.labnol.org/images/2008/pixel-painting.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx12/cdn85@2020_5/2020/08/17/16-46-08-883_7710c2170c2c649c.webp","https://www.labnol.org/images/2008/emoji-painting.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx15/cdn12@2020_6/2020/08/17/16-46-12-325_d326349e3788d55b.webp","https://www.labnol.org/images/2008/emoji-art.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx12/cdn51@2020_6/2020/08/17/16-46-11-363_4d430e6e7f10cb31.webp"}},{"createdTime":"2020-08-18 00:45:54","updatedTime":"2020-08-18 00:45:54","title":"How to Use Hyperlinks in Google Sheets","link":"https://www.labnol.org/code/google-sheets-hyperlinks-2006232","description":"<p>This guide explains how you can easily create and manage hyperlinks in Google Sheets. An entire cell in the sheet, or specific text inside the cell, can be linked to external web pages. A cell can also contain multiple hyperlinks.</p> \n<p>If you type a web page address in a Google Sheet cell, it is automatically converted into a clickable hyperlink.</p> \n<p><img src=\"https://www.labnol.org/419f48ad74aee051c6ec58baec31b0e2/link1.gif\" alt=\"Text converted into hyperlink\" /></p> \n<p>You can add anchor text to plain hyperlinks for more accessible URLs. Hover your mouse over the hyperlink and click the Edit icon. Now add the anchor text in the Text input box and click the green Apply button.</p> \n<p>Alternatively, you may use the built-in <code class=\"language-text\">HYPERLINK</code> function in Google Sheet to create web links with (optional) anchor text.</p> \n<div class=\"gatsby-highlight\" data-language=\"javascript\"> \n <pre class=\"language-javascript\"><code class=\"language-javascript\"> <span class=\"token operator\">=</span><span class=\"token constant\">HYPERLINK</span><span class=\"token punctuation\">(</span><span class=\"token string\">\"https://www.labnol.org\"</span><span class=\"token punctuation\">,</span> <span class=\"token string\">\"Digital Inspiration\"</span><span class=\"token punctuation\">)</span></code></pre> \n</div> \n<p><img src=\"https://www.labnol.org/cae24deebabb4379c325896d976d37ed/link2.gif\" alt=\"Add anchor text to hyperlink\" /></p> \n<p>It is also possible to include multiple hyperlinks inside a single cell of the Google Sheet.</p> \n<p>Just type any text, include URLs in plain text and when you move the cursor out of the cell, the URLs are converted into hyperlinks.</p> \n<p><strong>Bonus Tip:</strong> While a cell with multiple links is selected, press <code class=\"language-text\">Alt+Enter</code> and all the links with open at once in new tabs.</p> \n<p><img src=\"https://www.labnol.org/106f8b56543b52a124692409b9cbea2b/link3.gif\" alt=\"Multiple hyperlinks in Google Sheet Cell\" /></p> \n<p>You can use the previous technique to edit multiple hyperlinks contained in a single cell and add anchor text.</p> \n<p>Hover your mouse over a link in the cell, click the edit icon and change the Anchor text. Repeat this for all other links in the same cell.</p> \n<p><img src=\"https://www.labnol.org/cfd7cecc5295509a1bfb4f2e294edcb2/link4.gif\" alt=\"Format Muliple URLs\" /></p> \n<p>Also see <a Calendars","link":"https://www.labnol.org/add-to-calendar-link-generator-200623","description":"<p>You are organizing an online event - maybe a meeting on Zoom or a training session hosted on Google Meet - and you would like the attendees to add the event to their own calendars. Once added to their calendar, the event will act as an automatic reminder and attendees will get a notification when the conference is about to start.</p> \n<p>There are two way to go about this:</p> \n<ol> \n <li><p>You can create a new meeting in your online calendar (Google, Outlook or any other calendar) and add the individual attendees as guests so the event automatically gets added to their calendar as well.</p></li> \n <li><p>You can include an “Add to Calendar” link or button in your email messages, <a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/internet/file-upload-google-forms/29170/\">forms</a> and website pages. Anyone can click the link to quickly save your event on to their calendars - see <a href=\"https://calendar.google.com/calendar/render?action=TEMPLATE&amp;dates=20250630T223000Z%2F20250630T233000Z&amp;details=Use%20the%20%3Ca%20href%3D%22https%3A%2F%2Fbit.ly%2Fcalendarlinks%22%3EAdd%20to%20Calendar%3C%2Fa%3E%20app%20to%20create%20links%20that%20will%20let%20anyone%20save%20your%20events%20to%20their%20online%20calendars.%0A%0A%F0%9F%93%86%20%20https%3A%2F%2Fbit.ly%2Fcalendarlinks%0A%0A&amp;location=Digital%20Inspiration&amp;text=Add%20to%20Calendar\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">live demo</a>.</p></li> \n</ol> \n<h3 id=\"create-add-to-calendar-links-for-emails-and-websites\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/add-to-calendar-link-generator-200623#create-add-to-calendar-links-for-emails-and-websites\" aria-label=\"create add to calendar links for emails and websites permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>Create Add to Calendar Links for Emails and Websites</h3> \n<p>The <a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/apps/calendar.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">Add to Calendar</a> app can create links that will let people quickly save your events on to their own calendars. You can create links and event reminder buttons for Google Calendar, Outlook, Microsoft Office 365 and Yahoo! Calendar.</p> \n<p>The app will also generate downloadable iCalendar .ics files.</p> \n<p><span class=\"gatsby-resp-image-wrapper\" timezone of your event. Then use the built-in date and time picker to specify the event start date and end date. If the event spans the entire day, check the “All Day Event” option.</p> \n<p>The event description field can have long text, hyperlinks and simple HTML tags for formatting. Next choose the calendar name to target and click the Generate button. The app generates plain links that you can paste in emails and HTML buttons (with inline CSS) for embedding in your web pages and email newsletters.</p> \n<p>You can create “Add to Calendar” links on both the desktop and your mobile phone. class=\"gatsby-resp-image-wrapper\" style=\"position:relative;display:block;margin-left:auto;margin-right:auto;max-width:720px\"> <a class=\"gatsby-resp-image-link\" GraphQL Query\" src=\"https://www.labnol.org/static/a90b218077b200b2be617eca231d0459/16546/121918.png\" srcSet=\"/static/a90b218077b200b2be617eca231d0459/96042/121918.png 1080w,/static/a90b218077b200b2be617eca231d0459/33c03/121918.png 1140w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 720px) 100vw, 720px\" style=\"width:100%;height:100%;margin:0;vertical-align:middle;position:absolute;top:0;left:0\" loading=\"lazy\" /> </a> </span></p> \n<p>The GraphQL query filters all files that have mimeType of images and then compares the <code class=\"language-text\">relativePath</code> of the image with the fileName passed in the src props.</p> \n<p>If the file is found, it looks at the extension of the file. SVG images are served without optimization while all other <a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/software/tutorials/jpeg-vs-png-image-quality-or-bandwidth/5385/\">image formats</a> are served compressed and optimized.</p> \n<h3 id=\"step-5-embed-images-in-gatsby\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/code/gatsby-images-200607#step-5-embed-images-in-gatsby\" aria-label=\"step 5 embed images in gatsby permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>Step 5. Embed Images in Gatsby</h3> \n<p>Now copy the image that you wish to use in your React component / Gatsby page in the <code class=\"language-text\">images/</code> folder. Include the image in your component using the new Image tag.</p> \n<div class=\"gatsby-highlight\" data-language=\"javascript\"> \n <pre class=\"language-javascript\"><code all other attributes that are available with the HTML <code class=\"language-text\">&lt;img&gt;</code> tag.</p>","descriptionType":"html","publishedDate":"Sun, 07 Jun 2020 00:00:00 +0000","feedId":259,"bgimg":"https://www.labnol.org/static/0982cca8299da06d17de3704eeea8800/16546/121359.png","linkMd5":"1794b2ff4d9b9038d80563c4d6afe56f","bgimgJsdelivr":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx23/cdn5@2020_3/2020/08/17/16-46-08-763_9b36e190e61f1fba.webp","destWidth":720,"destHeight":419,"author":"","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://www.labnol.org/static/0982cca8299da06d17de3704eeea8800/16546/121359.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx23/cdn5@2020_3/2020/08/17/16-46-08-763_9b36e190e61f1fba.webp","https://www.labnol.org/static/a90b218077b200b2be617eca231d0459/16546/121918.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx20/cdn86@2020_6/2020/08/17/16-46-11-659_0a1676cc0ff70ca7.webp"}},{"createdTime":"2020-08-18 00:45:54","updatedTime":"2020-08-18 00:45:54","title":"How to Send Reminder Emails Based on Dates in Google Sheets","link":"https://www.labnol.org/send-reminder-emails-200425","description":"<p>John Q Public runs a travel agency and they have thousands of clients across the globe. Other than managing tickets and travel itineraries, the agency also keeps a record of passports and visas of their clients to ensure that customers have valid documents at the time of travel.</p> \n<p>Most countries require that a foreigner’s passport must be valid for at least six months from the date of entry. The US government, therefore, recommends that you renew your passport at least nine months before it expires.</p> \n<h2 id=\"send-automatic-emails-with-google-sheets\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/send-reminder-emails-200425#send-automatic-emails-with-google-sheets\" aria-label=\"send automatic emails with google sheets permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>Send Automatic Emails with Google Sheets</h2> \n<p>John’s agency is looking for a reminder system that will automatically send an email notification to their customers when their passports have expired or are due for renewal in the next few months. Let’s see how they can build such a workflow in 10 minutes with the help of <a href=\"https://gsuite.google.com/marketplace/app/mail_merge_with_attachments/223404411203\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">Mail Merge for Gmail</a>.</p> \n<p>The idea is simple.</p> \n<p>We have the customer data in a Google Sheet or a Microsoft Excel spreadsheet. The “Expiry Date” column in the spreadsheet contains the date when the passport is set to expire. We setup a cron job that runs in the background and monitors the expiry date. If any date in the sheet is less than, say, 12 months from today, an automatic email reminder is sent to the customer.</p> \n<h3 id=\"create-the-reminder-email-workflow\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/send-reminder-emails-200425#create-the-reminder-email-workflow\" aria-label=\"create the reminder email workflow permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>Create the Reminder Email Workflow</h3> \n<p>To get started, install the <a href=\"https://gsuite.google.com/marketplace/app/mail_merge_with_attachments/223404411203\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">Mail Merge for Gmail</a> add-on for Google Sheets. If you have never used the merge add-on earlier, please watch the <a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ChGBcFtYdVA\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">Mail Merge tutorial</a> for a quick overview.</p> \n<p><span class=\"gatsby-resp-image-wrapper\" style=\"position:relative;display:block;margin-left:auto;margin-right:auto;max-width:720px\"> <a class=\"gatsby-resp-image-link\" href=\"https://www.labnol.org/static/143608f3e875751f21077e640e168f0d/dd04a/mail-merge-sheet.png\" style=\"display:block\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\"> <span class=\"gatsby-resp-image-background-image\" style=\"padding-bottom:70%;position:relative;bottom:0;left:0;display:block\"></span> <img class=\"gatsby-resp-image-image\" alt=\"Email Reminders Sheet\" title=\"Email Reminders Sheet\" src=\"https://www.labnol.org/static/143608f3e875751f21077e640e168f0d/16546/mail-merge-sheet.png\" srcSet=\"/static/143608f3e875751f21077e640e168f0d/96042/mail-merge-sheet.png 180w,/static/143608f3e875751f21077e640e168f0d/7a322/mail-merge-sheet.png 360w,/static/143608f3e875751f21077e640e168f0d/16546/mail-merge-sheet.png 720w,/static/143608f3e875751f21077e640e168f0d/6d80e/mail-merge-sheet.png 1080w,/static/143608f3e875751f21077e640e168f0d/dd04a/mail-merge-sheet.png 1211w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 720px) 100vw, 720px\" style=\"width:100%;height:100%;margin:0;vertical-align:middle;position:absolute;top:0;left:0\" loading=\"lazy\" /> </a> </span></p> \n<p>Next, create a new Google Sheet and choose Addons &gt; Mail Merge with Attachments &gt; Create Merge Template. If you have your customer data in an Excel sheet, you can easily import the records into this Google sheet using the File &gt; Import menu.</p> \n<p>Next, we’ll use the <a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/internet/arrayformula-copy-formulas-in-entire-column/29711/\">Array Formulas</a> to populate the <code class=\"language-text\">Scheduled Date</code> column based on the date in the <code class=\"language-text\">Expiry Date</code> column. Go to row #2 of the scheduled date column and paste this formula:</p> \n<div class=\"gatsby-highlight\" data-language=\"text\"> \n <pre class=\"language-text\"><code class=\"language-text\">=ArrayFormula(IF(ISBLANK(E2:E),\"\",E2:E-365))</code></pre> \n</div> \n<p>The date in the <code class=\"language-text\">Scheduled Date</code> column will automatically be filled with a date that is 12 months before the date in the <code class=\"language-text\">Expiry Date</code> column. Thus if the passport expiration date is set to <code class=\"language-text\">July 12, 2021</code>, the follow-up reminder email would be sent exactly a year earlier on <code class=\"language-text\">July 12, 2020</code>.</p> \n<p><span class=\"gatsby-resp-image-wrapper\" style=\"position:relative;display:block;margin-left:auto;margin-right:auto;max-width:720px\"> <a class=\"gatsby-resp-image-link\" href=\"https://www.labnol.org/static/5086dce490b0a1679a10b900ca088979/498a6/send-email-reminders.png\" style=\"display:block\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\"> <span class=\"gatsby-resp-image-background-image\" 720px\" style=\"width:100%;height:100%;margin:0;vertical-align:middle;position:absolute;top:0;left:0\" loading=\"lazy\" /> </a> </span></p> \n<p>Open the Gmail website, compose a new email message that will be the reminder template and save it in your drafts folder. The email body and subject can include column titles, enclosed inside double-curly braces and these will be replaced with actual values from the Google Sheet when the email is sent.</p> \n<h4 id=\"auto-expiry-reminder-email\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/send-reminder-emails-200425#auto-expiry-reminder-email\" aria-label=\"auto expiry reminder email permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>Auto Expiry Reminder Email</h4> \n<p>Here’s how are sample reminder email template looks like. You can also include emojis, images, and file attachments in your email drafts.</p> \n<p><span class=\"gatsby-resp-image-wrapper\" Addons menu in the sheet and choose Configure Mail Merge.</p> \n<p>Here follow the step-by-step wizard to add your sender’s name and also specify addresses that you wish to CC/BCC in every merged message.</p> \n<p>In the Create Email Template section, choose “Use a Gmail Draft” and select the draft template that you’ve created in the previous step.</p> \n<h3 id=\"send-date-based-reminder-emails\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/send-reminder-emails-200425#send-date-based-reminder-emails\" aria-label=\"send date based reminder The speaker video and the slides appear side-by-side and, as the video progresses, the slides auto-change in sync with the video.</p> \n<p>You can try a <a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Axy6JQTJUUA\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">live demo</a> of SlideCasts <a href=\"https://talltweets.com/slidecast/?v=71mvp1fJx9A&amp;s=19xmmcaSpmD_LzYFSkiVMp_u1c9qjlWBCGYbhES-vjGw&amp;m=0,10,25,30,40,70,85,110\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">here</a>. Just hit the play button on the YouTube video and you’ll notice that the slides will change at the 10s, 25s and 30s mark (configurable).</p> \n<p>SlideCasts can be really useful for educators involved in remote teaching. The teacher’s “talking head” video can be uploaded to YouTube and the lecture slides can be hosted on Google Slides.</p> \n<p>If your course slides are available as a PowerPoint presentation that will work as well since you can directly upload your PPT and PPTX files to Google Slides.</p> \n<h3 id=\"how-to-sync-presentation-slides-with-video\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/software/sync-powerpoint-with-video/18768/#how-to-sync-presentation-slides-with-video\" aria-label=\"how to sync presentation slides with video permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>How to Sync Presentation Slides with Video</h3> \n<p><iframe width=\"100%\" height=\"315\" src=\"https://www.youtube-nocookie.com/embed/Axy6JQTJUUA?rel=0\" frameBorder=\"0\" allow=\"accelerometer; autoplay; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture\" allowfullscreen=\"\"></iframe></p> \n<p>The first step is to install <a href=\"https://gsuite.google.com/marketplace/app/creator_studio/509621243108\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">Creator Studio</a>. Next go to <a href=\"https://slides.google.com\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">slides.google.com</a> and open any existing presentation.</p> \n<p>Go to the Addons menu inside Slides, choose Creator Studio and then select Create Slidecasts. Here specify the URL of the YouTube video and your Google Slides deck (both should be public).</p> \n<p>Next, specify the timestamps in mm:ss format (minute seconds) when the slides should change in sync with the video.</p> \n<p>For instance, if you want the second slide to show at the 15s point in the video, the 3rd slide at the 45s mark and the 4th slide at 1 minute, 20 second mark, your markers would be written as:</p> \n<p><code class=\"language-text\">0, 15, 45, 1:20</code></p> \n<p>That’s pretty much it. Click the Generate button and copy-paste the HTML code into your website.</p> \n<p>The SlideCast player is responsive so the video and slides will auto-resize based on the size of the visitor’s screen.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://gsuite.google.com/marketplace/app/creator_studio/509621243108\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">Download Creator Studio</a></p> \n<p><span We’ll have a Google Sheet that will be the data source and have all the answer choices for various questions in the Google Form.</p> \n<p>The app will read the data from this Google Sheet and auto-populate the choices in the form with one click. You can even create a time-trigger that runs every hour, day or month to dynamically update your form using the most current data available in the spreadsheet.</p> \n<h3 id=\"add-options-in-dropdown-lists--multiple-choice-questions\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/code/google-forms-choices-from-sheets-200630#add-options-in-dropdown-lists--multiple-choice-questions\" aria-label=\"add options in dropdown lists  multiple choice questions permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>Add Options in Dropdown Lists &amp; Multiple Choice Questions</h3> \n<p>Create a Google Spreadsheet and add the question titles in the first row of the sheet, one per column. style=\"width:100%;height:100%;margin:0;vertical-align:middle;position:absolute;top:0;left:0\" loading=\"lazy\" /> </a> </span></p> \n<p>The important thing to note here is that your column headings in the spreadsheet should exactly match the form field labels of the Google Form. The Google Script can bulk add answers in multiple-choice questions with a single answer, drop-down lists and checkbox with multiple options.</p> \n<h4 id=\"bulk-add-question-choices-with-google-script\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/code/google-forms-choices-from-sheets-200630#bulk-add-question-choices-with-google-script\" aria-label=\"bulk add question choices with google script permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>Bulk Add Question Choices with Google Script</h4> \n<p>Open the Google Sheet that has the question choices, go to the Tools menu and choose Script Editor. Replace the default code in the script editor with the Google Script below. Please watch the <a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Z-gCwZ0lXd8\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">video tutorial</a> to know in more detail how this code works.</p> Go to the Run menu inside the Script editor, choose <code class=\"language-text\">populateGoogleForms</code> function and it should instantly choices for all the specified questions in the Google Form.</p> \n<h4 id=\"dynamically-update-answers-in-google-forms\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/code/google-forms-choices-from-sheets-200630#dynamically-update-answers-in-google-forms\" aria-label=\"dynamically update answers in google forms permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>Dynamically Update Answers in Google Forms</h4> \n<p>Going forward, whenever you need to update the answer choices in Google Forms, you can simply update the values inside the spreadsheet and run the same auto-populate function from the Script editor.</p> \n<p>Or, to make things even more simple, you can add a button on the spreadsheet page that, when clicked, will automatically update the answers in Google Forms for you.</p> \n<p>Go to the Insert menu in Google Sheets, choose drawing and pick any shape. You can also add overlay text to the shape. Once the shape is placed on the spreadsheet canvas, click the menu, choose assign script and type <code class=\"language-text\">populateGoogleForms</code>.</p> \n<p><img src=\"https://www.labnol.org/fbee3adfcb81f21d35a710bf65b76eda/google-sheets-button.gif\" alt=\"Bulk Import Button in Google Sheets\" /></p> \n<p>That’s it. You can click this button to update your Google Forms right within Google sheets. Do note that the script will not append choices, it will replace all existing choices with the ones that are available in your Google Sheet.</p> \n<p>Also see: <a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/prefilled-google-forms-200601\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">Send Pre-filled Google Forms via Email</a></p>","descriptionType":"html","publishedDate":"Tue, 30 Jun 2020 00:00:00 +0000","feedId":259,"bgimg":"https://www.labnol.org/static/034ad4265305ed827976eaf0dedc5a01/16546/google-sheet-form-answers.png","linkMd5":"b93b9609abc419e7ba556df830699613","bgimgJsdelivr":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx7/cdn1@2020_4/2020/08/17/16-46-08-903_3e980f040e5d6d03.webp","destWidth":720,"destHeight":649,"author":"","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://www.labnol.org/static/034ad4265305ed827976eaf0dedc5a01/16546/google-sheet-form-answers.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx7/cdn1@2020_4/2020/08/17/16-46-08-903_3e980f040e5d6d03.webp","https://www.labnol.org/fbee3adfcb81f21d35a710bf65b76eda/google-sheets-button.gif":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx10/cdn96@2020_2/2020/08/17/16-46-19-963_0e035fe1e2caef55.webp"}},{"createdTime":"2020-08-18 00:45:54","updatedTime":"2020-08-18 00:45:54","title":"How to Sell Digital Products Online with Google Drive and PayPal","link":"https://www.labnol.org/internet/sell-digital-products-online/28554/","description":"<p>The web has made it incredibly easy for anyone to sell digital products directly to customers through websites, social media, and email newsletters. You can sell PDF ebooks, event tickets, <a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/internet/sell-music-online/13403/\">MP3 music</a>, photos, gift cards, <a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/products\">software apps</a>, license keys, coupon codes, <a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/internet/html-website-templates/32059/\">website templates</a>, fonts, graphics, <a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/internet/learn-web-development/31945/\">video courses</a>, and many more downloadable files.</p> \n<p>While there are quite a few e-commerce platforms that help you sell digital products - Gumroad, E-junkie, Paddle, FastSpring,&nbsp;Shopify, Instamojo and WooCommerce, to name a few, &nbsp;here’s a do-it-yourself solution that will help you build your own online digital store in under 5 minutes using PayPal and your Google account.</p> \n<h2 id=\"sell-digital-goods---the-workflow\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/internet/sell-digital-products-online/28554/#sell-digital-goods---the-workflow\" aria-label=\"sell digital goods   the workflow permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>Sell Digital Goods - The Workflow</h2> \n<p>Before we get into the implementation, here’s an overview of how the payment and digital delivery workflow works.</p> \n<ol> \n <li>Embed the “Buy Now” buttons into your website or blog.</li> \n <li>The buyer clicks the checkout button, enters their credit card details and completes the payment. The customer stays on your site and isn’t redirected anywhere to complete the purchase.</li> \n <li>The order is delivered to the customer from your Gmail in a personalized email message. You can also attach a tax invoice in the confirmation email.</li> \n</ol> \n<p>You can head over to the&nbsp;<a href=\"https://digitalgoods.dev/paypal/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">live demo</a>&nbsp;page and experience the 1-step checkout experience on your desktop or mobile phone.</p> \n<h2 id=\"sell-digital-downloads-with-paypal-and-google-drive\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/internet/sell-digital-products-online/28554/#sell-digital-downloads-with-paypal-and-google-drive\" aria-label=\"sell digital downloads with paypal and google drive permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>Sell Digital Downloads with PayPal and Google Drive</h2> \n<p>The workflow uses Google Drive for securely hosting files, PayPal for processing payments, Google Sheets for generating professional PDF invoices and Gmail for delivering the order to the buyer as file attachments.</p> \n<p>There are no limitations on the size of files or the number of products that you can sell. There are no bandwidth or storage restrictions. There’s no transaction fee except for the payment processing fees that are charged directly by PayPal and Stripe.</p> \n<p><iframe width=\"100%\" height=\"315\" \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 Started Selling Digital Goods</h2> \n<p>Here’s a step-by-step <a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=kbb-YViCJBM\" title=\"How to Sell Digital Goods with PayPal\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow href=\"https://www.labnol.org/internet/sell-digital-products-online/28554/#step-1-create-a-paypal-app\" aria-label=\"step 1 create a paypal app permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>Step 1: Create a PayPal App</h3> \n<p>Go to <a href=\"https://www.paypal.com/signin?returnUri=https%3A%2F%2Fdeveloper.paypal.com%2Fdeveloper%2Fapplications\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">developer.paypal.com</a> and sign-in with your PayPal account. If you don’t have one, <a href=\"https://www.paypal.com/us/webapps/mpp/account-selection\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">sign-up here</a> for a new Business account.</p> \n<p>Inside your PayPal developer dashboard, go to <code class=\"language-text\">My Apps &amp; Credentials</code>, and create a <a href=\"https://developer.paypal.com/developer/applications/create\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">new app</a> under the <code class=\"language-text\">Rest API Apps</code> section. You can give your app any name as it is for internal use only. You need to create client credentials for both Sandbox and Live mode.</p> \n<h3 id=\"step-2-create-a-paypal-webhook\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/internet/sell-digital-products-online/28554/#step-2-create-a-paypal-webhook\" aria-label=\"step 2 create a paypal webhook permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>Step 2: Create a PayPal Webhook</h3> \n<p>When a buyer completes the purchase and makes the payment, PayPal will send your Google Sheets a notification by calling a specific URL and this is known as a webhook.</p> \n<p>To create a webhook, go to <a href=\"https://digitalgoods.dev/copy\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">digitalgoods.dev/copy</a> and copy the Google Sheet to your Google Drive. Inside the sheet, go to <em>Tools &gt; Script Editor</em>,&nbsp;then choose <em>Publish &gt; Deploy As Web App</em> and click the Update button to create your PayPal webhook. Copy the URL to the clipboard.</p> \n<p>You will have to authorize the script once since it has to do all the operations - send emails, attach Drive files, generate PDF invoices - on behalf of your Google Account.</p> \n<h3 id=\"step-3-configure-app-inside-google-sheet\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/internet/sell-digital-products-online/28554/#step-3-configure-app-inside-google-sheet\" aria-label=\"step 3 configure app inside google sheet permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>Step 3: Configure App inside Google Sheet</h3> \n<p>Switch to the “Configuration” sheet inside the Google Spreadsheet and paste the webhook URL inside the “webhook” field. Next, copy-paste the Client ID and Secret generated in step 1 inside the corresponding fields of the Google Sheet.</p> \n<p><span class=\"gatsby-resp-image-wrapper\" style=\"position:relative;display:block;margin-left:auto;margin-right:auto;max-width:720px\"> <a class=\"gatsby-resp-image-link\" href=\"https://www.labnol.org/static/bc1d43a374771cdd5e379d6c528e243a/6e6b4/paypal-app-configuration.png\" style=\"display:block\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\"> <span class=\"gatsby-resp-image-background-image\" style=\"padding-bottom:56.666666666666664%;position:relative;bottom:0;left:0;display:block\"></span> <img class=\"gatsby-resp-image-image\" alt=\"paypal-app-configuration.png\" title=\"paypal-app-configuration.png\" src=\"https://www.labnol.org/static/bc1d43a374771cdd5e379d6c528e243a/16546/paypal-app-configuration.png\" srcSet=\"/static/bc1d43a374771cdd5e379d6c528e243a/96042/paypal-app-configuration.png 180w,/static/bc1d43a374771cdd5e379d6c528e243a/7a322/paypal-app-configuration.png 360w,/static/bc1d43a374771cdd5e379d6c528e243a/16546/paypal-app-configuration.png 720w,/static/bc1d43a374771cdd5e379d6c528e243a/6d80e/paypal-app-configuration.png 1080w,/static/bc1d43a374771cdd5e379d6c528e243a/6e6b4/paypal-app-configuration.png 1400w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 720px) 100vw, 720px\" style=\"width:100%;height:100%;margin:0;vertical-align:middle;position:absolute;top:0;left:0\" loading=\"lazy\" /> </a> </span></p> \n<p>There are few other mandatory fields in the sheet. Choose your default currency, the shipping preference (whether you want to capture the address on the buyer), specify your brand name and the soft descriptor (this will show in the credit card statement of the buyer).</p> \n<p>Go to the Digital Goods menu in the sheet (it is near the <em>Help</em> menu) and choose Test PayPal Configuration to verify if the PayPal and Google Sheets connection is working.</p> \n<h3 id=\"step-4-add-your-digital-products\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/internet/sell-digital-products-online/28554/#step-4-add-your-digital-products\" aria-label=\"step 4 add your digital products permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>Step 4: Add your Digital Products</h3> \n<p>Switch to the “Items” sheet and enter the default tax rate in the cell E1. Next, add one or more products in the sheet, one per row. You only need to specify the price of the item in column D, the Tax and Total Amount is automatically calculated based on the tax rate set in E1.</p> \n<p><span class=\"gatsby-resp-image-wrapper\" style=\"position:relative;display:block;margin-left:auto;margin-right:auto;max-width:720px\"> <a class=\"gatsby-resp-image-link\" href=\"https://www.labnol.org/static/a07567b50ea211149e5e1b4c174650e3/f3787/paypal-digital-products.png\" style=\"display:block\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\"> <span class=\"gatsby-resp-image-background-image\" style=\"padding-bottom:70.55555555555556%;position:relative;bottom:0;left:0;display:block\"></span> <img class=\"gatsby-resp-image-image\" alt=\"PayPal Digital Products\" title=\"PayPal Digital Products\" src=\"https://www.labnol.org/static/a07567b50ea211149e5e1b4c174650e3/16546/paypal-digital-products.png\" srcSet=\"/static/a07567b50ea211149e5e1b4c174650e3/96042/paypal-digital-products.png 180w,/static/a07567b50ea211149e5e1b4c174650e3/7a322/paypal-digital-products.png 360w,/static/a07567b50ea211149e5e1b4c174650e3/16546/paypal-digital-products.png 720w,/static/a07567b50ea211149e5e1b4c174650e3/6d80e/paypal-digital-products.png 1080w,/static/a07567b50ea211149e5e1b4c174650e3/f3787/paypal-digital-products.png 1130w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 720px) 100vw, 720px\" style=\"width:100%;height:100%;margin:0;vertical-align:middle;position:absolute;top:0;left:0\" loading=\"lazy\" /> </a> </span></p> \n<p>To attach files to your digital product, highlight the cell in the Files column, then go to the <em>Digital Goods</em> menu and choose <em>Attach Drive Files</em>. It opens the Google File picker and you can select one or more files from your Google Drive that will be sent to the buyer after they purchase the corresponding product.</p> \n<h3 id=\"step-4-create-the-tax-invoice-template\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/internet/sell-digital-products-online/28554/#step-4-create-the-tax-invoice-template\" aria-label=\"step 4 create the tax invoice template permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>Step 4: Create the Tax Invoice Template</h3> \n<p>Switch to the “Invoice” sheet and customize the invoice template. You can use formulas, add your logos, apply styles to match your brand and the template would be converted to a PDF file and sent as a file attachment in the order confirmation emails.</p> \n<p><span class=\"gatsby-resp-image-wrapper\" style=\"position:relative;display:block;margin-left:auto;margin-right:auto;max-width:720px\"> <a class=\"gatsby-resp-image-link\" href=\"https://www.labnol.org/static/d98a79c11dccbf88b5b622eb16f27456/adf4c/paypal-pdf-invoice.png\" style=\"display:block\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\"> <span class=\"gatsby-resp-image-background-image\" style=\"padding-bottom:99.44444444444443%;position:relative;bottom:0;left:0;display:block\"></span> <img class=\"gatsby-resp-image-image\" alt=\"paypal-pdf-invoice.png\" title=\"paypal-pdf-invoice.png\" src=\"https://www.labnol.org/static/d98a79c11dccbf88b5b622eb16f27456/16546/paypal-pdf-invoice.png\" srcSet=\"/static/d98a79c11dccbf88b5b622eb16f27456/96042/paypal-pdf-invoice.png 180w,/static/d98a79c11dccbf88b5b622eb16f27456/7a322/paypal-pdf-invoice.png 360w,/static/d98a79c11dccbf88b5b622eb16f27456/16546/paypal-pdf-invoice.png 720w,/static/d98a79c11dccbf88b5b622eb16f27456/adf4c/paypal-pdf-invoice.png 855w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 720px) 100vw, 720px\" style=\"width:100%;height:100%;margin:0;vertical-align:middle;position:absolute;top:0;left:0\" loading=\"lazy\" /> </a> </span></p> \n<p>The invoice template can include place markers, similar to the ones you have used inside <a href=\"https://gsuite.google.com/marketplace/app/document_studio/429444628321\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">Document Studio</a>. For instance, the {{Name}} variable will be replaced with the full name of the customer as found in the PayPal order. The {{Email}} variable is replaced with the buyer’s email address while the {{Invoice Id}} adds a unique invoice number to your invoice.</p> \n<h3 id=\"step-5-create-the-order-confirmation-email\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/internet/sell-digital-products-online/28554/#step-5-create-the-order-confirmation-email\" aria-label=\"step 5 create the order confirmation email permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>Step 5: Create the Order Confirmation Email</h3> \n<p>Switch to the “Email” sheet and create the HTML template that will be sent to customers after they complete the payment. The email will automatically include the files and PDF invoice as attachments but you can customize the email message and subject.</p> \n<p>The first row in the sheet is the subject and everything else will go in the message body. The emails, like&nbsp;<a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/software/mail-merge-with-gmail/13289/\">Mail Merge</a>,&nbsp;can be personalized and you can also use <a href=\"https://htmlmail.pro/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">HTML tags</a> to add images, links and rich content in the emails.</p> \n<h3 id=\"step-6-test-your-paypal-buttons\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/internet/sell-digital-products-online/28554/#step-6-test-your-paypal-buttons\" aria-label=\"step 6 test your paypal buttons permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>Step 6: Test your PayPal buttons</h3> \n<p>Now that you have added the products to the Google Sheet, it is time to test the integration in sandbox mode before you embed the buttons on your live website.</p> \n<p>Go back to your <a href=\"https://developer.paypal.com/developer/applications/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">PayPal dashboard</a>, and choose <code class=\"language-text\">Credit Card Generator</code> in the right sidebar under the Mock section. Here you can generate random credit card numbers with expiration date and CVV for testing your PayPal checkout buttons in sandbox mode.</p> \n<p>Inside the Google Sheet, choose <em>Digital Tools</em> &gt; <em>Embed PayPal Buttons</em>&nbsp;to generate the HTML embed code for your digital products. The screen offers embed codes in both the live and sandbox mode.</p> \n<p><span class=\"gatsby-resp-image-wrapper\" style=\"position:relative;display:block;margin-left:auto;margin-right:auto;max-width:720px\"> <a class=\"gatsby-resp-image-link\" href=\"https://www.labnol.org/static/9f57233afcb7fc225c3ed3f4f6834dfb/49d2b/embed-paypal-buttons.png\" style=\"display:block\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\"> <span class=\"gatsby-resp-image-background-image\" style=\"padding-bottom:81.11111111111111%;position:relative;bottom:0;left:0;display:block\"></span> <img class=\"gatsby-resp-image-image\" alt=\"embed-paypal-buttons.png\" title=\"embed-paypal-buttons.png\" src=\"https://www.labnol.org/static/9f57233afcb7fc225c3ed3f4f6834dfb/16546/embed-paypal-buttons.png\" srcSet=\"/static/9f57233afcb7fc225c3ed3f4f6834dfb/96042/embed-paypal-buttons.png 180w,/static/9f57233afcb7fc225c3ed3f4f6834dfb/7a322/embed-paypal-buttons.png 360w,/static/9f57233afcb7fc225c3ed3f4f6834dfb/16546/embed-paypal-buttons.png 720w,/static/9f57233afcb7fc225c3ed3f4f6834dfb/49d2b/embed-paypal-buttons.png 1046w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 720px) 100vw, 720px\" style=\"width:100%;height:100%;margin:0;vertical-align:middle;position:absolute;top:0;left:0\" loading=\"lazy\" /> </a> </span></p> \n<p>Click the Try button next to the Sandbox mode and you’ll be able to test the buttons right inside the Google Sheet. Click the credit card icon, enter the mock credit card number and click “Pay Now” to complete the test transaction.</p> \n<p>PayPal invokes the Webhook and it triggers the order workflow. Switch to the “Logs” sheet and you’ll soon find a new entry for the transaction that you just completed. Open your <a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/topic/gmail/\">Gmail</a> Sent items folder and you’ll find a copy of the email that was just sent the buyer’s email.</p> \n<p>If your integration is working as expected, go to the <em>Embed PayPal</em> menu in the sheet and this time copy the embed code for the “Live” mode and paste it on your website. Your product is now live and anyone in the world can buy your product with a single-step checkout.</p> \n<p>Here’s a sample email that will go out to customers after the purchase.</p> \n<p><span class=\"gatsby-resp-image-wrapper\" style=\"position:relative;display:block;margin-left:auto;margin-right:auto;max-width:720px\"> <a class=\"gatsby-resp-image-link\" href=\"https://www.labnol.org/static/119a74e372a7b0be28e6a5b3e1a3df20/f9002/order-confirmation-email.png\" style=\"display:block\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\"> <span class=\"gatsby-resp-image-background-image\" style=\"padding-bottom:86.1111111111111%;position:relative;bottom:0;left:0;display:block\"></span> <img class=\"gatsby-resp-image-image\" alt=\"order-confirmation-email.png\" title=\"order-confirmation-email.png\" src=\"https://www.labnol.org/static/119a74e372a7b0be28e6a5b3e1a3df20/16546/order-confirmation-email.png\" srcSet=\"/static/119a74e372a7b0be28e6a5b3e1a3df20/96042/order-confirmation-email.png 180w,/static/119a74e372a7b0be28e6a5b3e1a3df20/7a322/order-confirmation-email.png 360w,/static/119a74e372a7b0be28e6a5b3e1a3df20/16546/order-confirmation-email.png 720w,/static/119a74e372a7b0be28e6a5b3e1a3df20/f9002/order-confirmation-email.png 912w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 720px) 100vw, 720px\" style=\"width:100%;height:100%;margin:0;vertical-align:middle;position:absolute;top:0;left:0\" loading=\"lazy\" /> </a> </span></p> \n<p>All the incoming orders can be tracked in real-time inside the “Sales” tab of the Google Sheet. The sheet includes the customer’s name, email address, the order summary, and the buyer’s postal address. The address is only available if you have set the shipping preference in the configuration sheet to “GET_FROM_FILE”.</p> \n<p>You can directly run&nbsp;<a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/internet/personalized-mail-merge-in-gmail/20981/\">Mail Merge with Gmail</a>&nbsp;inside this sheet to easily send product updates to existing customers. If you have been using PayPal before switching to <a href=\"https://digitalgoods.dev\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">Digital Goods</a>, put all the PayPal emails under a new Gmail label, <a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/internet/extract-gmail-addresses/28037/\">extract the email addresses</a>&nbsp;inside the sheet and use that list for your merge.</p> \n<h3 id=\"how-to-sell-unique-license-keys--codes\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/internet/sell-digital-products-online/28554/#how-to-sell-unique-license-keys--codes\" aria-label=\"how to sell unique license keys  codes permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>How to Sell Unique License Keys &amp; Codes</h3> \n<p>In some businesses, you may want to send unique codes to the customer. These may include license numbers to unlock software apps (like we do at <a href=\"https://digitalinspiration.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">Digital Inspiration</a>), &nbsp;passwords to access streaming video courses, discount coupons, gift cards, event registration numbers and more.</p> \n<p><span class=\"gatsby-resp-image-wrapper\" style=\"position:relative;display:block;margin-left:auto;margin-right:auto;max-width:720px\"> <a class=\"gatsby-resp-image-link\" href=\"https://www.labnol.org/static/a63a12360defa3c061e8706dd5e72ebd/e0774/software-license-codes.png\" style=\"display:block\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\"> <span class=\"gatsby-resp-image-background-image\" style=\"padding-bottom:86.1111111111111%;position:relative;bottom:0;left:0;display:block\"></span> <img class=\"gatsby-resp-image-image\" alt=\"software-license-codes.png\" title=\"software-license-codes.png\" src=\"https://www.labnol.org/static/a63a12360defa3c061e8706dd5e72ebd/16546/software-license-codes.png\" srcSet=\"/static/a63a12360defa3c061e8706dd5e72ebd/96042/software-license-codes.png 180w,/static/a63a12360defa3c061e8706dd5e72ebd/7a322/software-license-codes.png 360w,/static/a63a12360defa3c061e8706dd5e72ebd/16546/software-license-codes.png 720w,/static/a63a12360defa3c061e8706dd5e72ebd/e0774/software-license-codes.png 860w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 720px) 100vw, 720px\" style=\"width:100%;height:100%;margin:0;vertical-align:middle;position:absolute;top:0;left:0\" loading=\"lazy\" /> </a> </span></p> \n<p>You can easily send unique license code with Digital Goods. Open the “Codes” sheet in the spreadsheet and put the pre-generated list of codes in one of the columns. Give this column a title as shown in the screenshot above. Next, include the {{column title}} in your email message and a unique code will be added in place of the marker.</p> \n<p>Internally, the app looks at the last row of the Sale sheet (the current order), fetches the codes from that same row in the Codes sheet and adds them to your email and invoice.</p> \n<h2 id=\"troubleshooting-tips\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/internet/sell-digital-products-online/28554/#troubleshooting-tips\" aria-label=\"troubleshooting tips permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>Troubleshooting Tips</h2> \n<p>The&nbsp;<a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=kbb-YViCJBM\" title=\"How to Sell Digital Goods with PayPal\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">video tutorial</a>&nbsp;explains the entire workflow in great detail but if you are still facing any issues, here are some tips:</p> \n<ol> \n <li>Go to the configuration sheet and set “yes” for the debug setting. href=\"https://www.labnol.org/embed/google/photos/\">Embed Google Photos</a>&nbsp;is a new web app that, as the name suggests, makes it extremely easy for you to pick any image hosted on Google Photos href=\"https://www.labnol.org/embed/google/photos/\">j.mp/EmbedGooglePhotos</a>, paste that link and it will instantly generate the embed code for your selected picture.</li> \n</ul> \n<p>That’s it. Open your website template, paste the generated code and save (<a href=\"http://jsbin.com/rusujov/edit?html,output\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener noreferrer\">see sample</a>). The image will now serve directly from your Google Photos account. \n<p>When you share any single photo in Google Photos, it creates an unlisted link that is accessible to anyone including those who are not logged into their Google Accounts. Internally, the embed app downloads the page behind this link and extracts the Open Graph tags to determine the direct link of the image and the underlying photo album.</p> \n<h3 id=\"change-height-and-width-of-the-image\" style=\"position:relative\"><a href=\"https://www.labnol.org/internet/embed-google-photos-in-website/29194/#change-height-and-width-of-the-image\" aria-label=\"change height and width of the image permalink\" class=\"anchor before\"> \n  <svg aria-hidden=\"true\" focusable=\"false\" height=\"16\" version=\"1.1\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" width=\"16\"> \n   <path fill-rule=\"evenodd\" d=\"M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z\"></path> \n  </svg></a>Change Height and Width of the Image</h3> \n<p>All images hosted inside Google Photos have a URL in a particular format:</p> \n<p><code class=\"language-text\">https://lh3.googleusercontent.com/xyz=w2400</code></p> \n<p>The w2400 in the URL indicates that the maximum width of the image will be 2400 pixels. However, if you have a higher resolution image, you can change the width parameter to something like w8000 meaning 8000 px wide. The height will be adjusted automatically to preserve the original aspect ratio.</p> \n<p>You can also specify the height and width values in the URL and Google Photos will fit the image to the specified size.</p> \n<p><code class=\"language-text\">https://lh3.googleusercontent.com/xyz=w1415-h944</code></p> \n<p>The embed app only works for single images and not albums.
